## Instruction

Today we have 3 new employees joining us, and each employee's information is stored in the Snowflake database.

Based on the employee's group assignment and training manual, automatically generate training task lists, send emails to the employee's email address, and update the task content and planned completion dates to the database.

For new employees, send onboarding emails in the following format:

```
Dear xxx, You have the following training tasks to complete:
xxx
xxx
xxx
Please complete them as soon as possible.
```

Additionally, you need to check for employee records where the current date has exceeded the training completion deadline but the task status is still "incomplete", send reminder emails to the employees themselves in the same format.

The order of the tasks in the email should be based on the order in the training manual.

And remember to CC their direct supervisor.

## Initial State

### Snowflake

You can view the database build process [here](https://github.com/hkust-nlp/mcpbench_dev/tree/release_v1/tasks/finalpool/landing-task-reminder/preprocess).

```json arguments
{
	"query": "\nSELECT e.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	e.NAME,
	e.EMAIL,
	e.REPORT_TO_ID,
	\n       CASE WHEN bt.EMPLOYEE_ID IS NOT NULL THEN 'Backend'\n            WHEN ft.EMPLOYEE_ID IS NOT NULL THEN 'Frontend'\n            WHEN dt.EMPLOYEE_ID IS NOT NULL THEN 'Data'\n            WHEN tt.EMPLOYEE_ID IS NOT NULL THEN 'Testing'\n            ELSE 'Unknown' END as GROUP_TYPE\nFROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE e\nLEFT JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT EMPLOYEE_ID FROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_BACKEND) bt ON e.EMPLOYEE_ID = bt.EMPLOYEE_ID\nLEFT JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT EMPLOYEE_ID FROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_FRONTEND) ft ON e.EMPLOYEE_ID = ft.EMPLOYEE_ID\nLEFT JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT EMPLOYEE_ID FROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_DATA) dt ON e.EMPLOYEE_ID = dt.EMPLOYEE_ID\nLEFT JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT EMPLOYEE_ID FROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_TESTING) tt ON e.EMPLOYEE_ID = tt.EMPLOYEE_ID\nWHERE e.REPORT_TO_ID IN (8001,
	8002,
	8003)\nORDER BY e.REPORT_TO_ID,
	e.EMPLOYEE_ID\n"
}
```

```json arguments
{
	"query": "\nSELECT pt.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	pt.TASK_NAME,
	pt.CREATE_DATE,
	\n       ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY pt.EMPLOYEE_ID ORDER BY pt.CREATE_DATE,
	pt.TASK_NAME) as TASK_ORDER\nFROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.PUBLIC_TASKS pt\nWHERE pt.EMPLOYEE_ID IN (6001,
	6002,
	6003)\nORDER BY pt.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	TASK_ORDER\n"
}
```

```json arguments
{
	"query": "\n-- Get all overdue tasks for each employee with supervisor info\nSELECT \n    e.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	\n    e.NAME,
	\n    e.EMAIL,
	\n    e.REPORT_TO_ID,
	\n    sup.EMAIL as SUPERVISOR_EMAIL,
	\n    pt.TASK_NAME,
	\n    pt.DDL,
	\n    'Public' as TASK_TYPE,
	\n    1 as TYPE_ORDER\nFROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.PUBLIC_TASKS pt\nJOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE e ON pt.EMPLOYEE_ID = e.EMPLOYEE_ID\nLEFT JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE sup ON e.REPORT_TO_ID = sup.EMPLOYEE_ID\nWHERE pt.FINISHED_FLAG = false AND pt.DDL < CURRENT_DATE()\n\nUNION ALL\n\nSELECT \n    e.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	\n    e.NAME,
	\n    e.EMAIL,
	\n    e.REPORT_TO_ID,
	\n    sup.EMAIL as SUPERVISOR_EMAIL,
	\n    bt.TASK_NAME,
	\n    bt.DDL,
	\n    'Backend' as TASK_TYPE,
	\n    2 as TYPE_ORDER\nFROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_BACKEND bt\nJOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE e ON bt.EMPLOYEE_ID = e.EMPLOYEE_ID\nLEFT JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE sup ON e.REPORT_TO_ID = sup.EMPLOYEE_ID\nWHERE bt.FINISHED_FLAG = false AND bt.DDL < CURRENT_DATE()\n\nUNION ALL\n\nSELECT \n    e.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	\n    e.NAME,
	\n    e.EMAIL,
	\n    e.REPORT_TO_ID,
	\n    sup.EMAIL as SUPERVISOR_EMAIL,
	\n    ft.TASK_NAME,
	\n    ft.DDL,
	\n    'Frontend' as TASK_TYPE,
	\n    2 as TYPE_ORDER\nFROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_FRONTEND ft\nJOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE e ON ft.EMPLOYEE_ID = e.EMPLOYEE_ID\nLEFT JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE sup ON e.REPORT_TO_ID = sup.EMPLOYEE_ID\nWHERE ft.FINISHED_FLAG = false AND ft.DDL < CURRENT_DATE()\n\nUNION ALL\n\nSELECT \n    e.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	\n    e.NAME,
	\n    e.EMAIL,
	\n    e.REPORT_TO_ID,
	\n    sup.EMAIL as SUPERVISOR_EMAIL,
	\n    dt.TASK_NAME,
	\n    dt.DDL,
	\n    'Data' as TASK_TYPE,
	\n    2 as TYPE_ORDER\nFROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_DATA dt\nJOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE e ON dt.EMPLOYEE_ID = e.EMPLOYEE_ID\nLEFT JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE sup ON e.REPORT_TO_ID = sup.EMPLOYEE_ID\nWHERE dt.FINISHED_FLAG = false AND dt.DDL < CURRENT_DATE()\n\nUNION ALL\n\nSELECT \n    e.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	\n    e.NAME,
	\n    e.EMAIL,
	\n    e.REPORT_TO_ID,
	\n    sup.EMAIL as SUPERVISOR_EMAIL,
	\n    tt.TASK_NAME,
	\n    tt.DDL,
	\n    'Testing' as TASK_TYPE,
	\n    2 as TYPE_ORDER\nFROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_TESTING tt\nJOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE e ON tt.EMPLOYEE_ID = e.EMPLOYEE_ID\nLEFT JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE sup ON e.REPORT_TO_ID = sup.EMPLOYEE_ID\nWHERE tt.FINISHED_FLAG = false AND tt.DDL < CURRENT_DATE()\n\nORDER BY EMPLOYEE_ID,
	TYPE_ORDER,
	TASK_NAME\n"
}
```

```json arguments
{
	"query": "\n-- Verify new employee tasks were created\nSELECT el.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	e.NAME,
	el.LANDING_TASK_ASSIGNED,
	\n       COUNT(DISTINCT pt.TASK_NAME) as PUBLIC_TASKS,
	\n       COUNT(DISTINCT COALESCE(bt.TASK_NAME,
	ft.TASK_NAME,
	dt.TASK_NAME,
	tt.TASK_NAME)) as GROUP_TASKS\nFROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE_LANDING el\nJOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE e ON el.EMPLOYEE_ID = e.EMPLOYEE_ID\nLEFT JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.PUBLIC_TASKS pt ON el.EMPLOYEE_ID = pt.EMPLOYEE_ID\nLEFT JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_BACKEND bt ON el.EMPLOYEE_ID = bt.EMPLOYEE_ID\nLEFT JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_FRONTEND ft ON el.EMPLOYEE_ID = ft.EMPLOYEE_ID\nLEFT JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_DATA dt ON el.EMPLOYEE_ID = dt.EMPLOYEE_ID\nLEFT JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_TESTING tt ON el.EMPLOYEE_ID = tt.EMPLOYEE_ID\nWHERE el.EMPLOYEE_ID IN (9001,
	9002,
	9003)\nGROUP BY el.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	e.NAME,
	el.LANDING_TASK_ASSIGNED\nORDER BY el.EMPLOYEE_ID\n"
}

```

<div className="tool-details">
```json arguments
{
	"query":"WITH OverdueTasks AS (\n    -- Public tasks\n    SELECT pt.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	e.NAME,
	e.EMAIL,
	e.REPORT_TO_ID,
	s.EMAIL as SUPERVISOR_EMAIL,
	pt.TASK_NAME,
	pt.DDL\n    FROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.PUBLIC_TASKS pt\n    JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE e ON pt.EMPLOYEE_ID = e.EMPLOYEE_ID\n    JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE s ON e.REPORT_TO_ID = s.EMPLOYEE_ID\n    WHERE pt.FINISHED_FLAG = false \n    AND pt.DDL < CURRENT_DATE()\n    \n    UNION ALL\n    \n    -- Group tasks\n    SELECT gt.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	e.NAME,
	e.EMAIL,
	e.REPORT_TO_ID,
	s.EMAIL as SUPERVISOR_EMAIL,
	gt.TASK_NAME,
	gt.DDL\n    FROM (\n        SELECT EMPLOYEE_ID,
	TASK_NAME,
	DDL FROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_FRONTEND\n        UNION ALL\n        SELECT EMPLOYEE_ID,
	TASK_NAME,
	DDL FROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_BACKEND\n        UNION ALL\n        SELECT EMPLOYEE_ID,
	TASK_NAME,
	DDL FROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_DATA\n        UNION ALL\n        SELECT EMPLOYEE_ID,
	TASK_NAME,
	DDL FROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_TESTING\n    ) gt\n    JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE e ON gt.EMPLOYEE_ID = e.EMPLOYEE_ID\n    JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE s ON e.REPORT_TO_ID = s.EMPLOYEE_ID\n    WHERE gt.DDL < CURRENT_DATE()\n)\nSELECT EMPLOYEE_ID,
	NAME,
	EMAIL,
	SUPERVISOR_EMAIL,
	\n       LISTAGG(TASK_NAME || ' (Due: ' || TO_CHAR(DDL,
	'YYYY-MM-DD') || ')',
	'\\n- ') WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY TASK_NAME) as TASK_LIST\nFROM OverdueTasks\nGROUP BY EMPLOYEE_ID,
	NAME,
	EMAIL,
	SUPERVISOR_EMAIL"
}

```
